Where players build a community, train troops, and attack other enemy to earn gold, elixir. \r\nThere are three currencies or resources in the game. Gold and elixir can be used to build and reload defenses that protect the player from other players’ attacks. Gems are the premium currency that helps to speed constructions or substitute other currency. \r\n\r\nThe game also features two single player campaign in which the player can attack a series of fortified enemy castles and earn gold and elixir. Attacks mode allow the player to loot gold, elixir and have a maximum timed length of 5 minutes.\r\nYou can also choose to play tower defend style to stop waves of attacking militias. \r\n\r\n\r\nBuildings\r\nThe game has 1 ’builders’ by default, but the player can install more builders (maximum 4) by buying them at an increasing number of gems. There are a number of buildings available to the player to defend their village, including cannons, heavy bow, archer towers. Players can also build walls, which can be upgraded as a player’s town hall level increases.\r\n\r\nResources\r\nTo earn and store gold and elixir, players must build gold mines and gold storages and elixir collectors and elixir storages, respectively. This creates more access routes for our brains to get at the desired information, and thus increases ease of recall.
